I call on Lebanese to reject all that affects our national unity and their dreams of a better tomorrow negatively
We support all democratic reforms in the region and all arab causes, especially the Palestinian cause, while rejecting naturalisation
We must encourage Lebanese expatriates to participate in our political life, and strengthen their bonds to their home country
We must question through dialogue whether our problems lie within our constitution and laws or in their application and fix those gaps
We must respect the dialogue table's decisions regarding disarming palestinians and our commitment to the international tribunal
We established diplomatic relations with Syria, passed the oil&gas law, are working on a just election law and one for regaining citizenship
For the first time since 1975, we have no external foreign forces on our lands, friend or enemy, and no internal conflicts for 3 years
Economic growth, social equality and basic health and financial aid for citizens in need are also prerequisites for any independent state
The conditions for Independence are freedom from foreign occupation and the extension of the state's authority over its entire territory
We remember today the united leadership of 1943 and the National Pact that put Lebanon above any foreign allegiances to the East or West
